<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>
<s> even genius itself attended these gatherings now and then with its nose on one side and june always introduced it to her father <\s>
<s> this she felt was exceptionally good for him for genius was a natural symptom he had never had fond as she was of him <\s>
<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>
<s> jolyon's native tenacity was roused and in the studio that evening he developed his objections <\s>
<s> he had never had any boils and his own teeth would last his time <\s>
<s> of course june admitted they would last his time if he didn't have them out <\s>
<s> but if he had more teeth he would have a better heart and his time would be longer <\s>

<s> he ought to be fighting <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>

<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>

<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>

<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> this is very dull for them <\s>

<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>

<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>
<s> according to june it was foolish and even cowardly to hide the past from jon <\s>
<s> sheer opportunism she called it <\s>

<s> and that was all she got from him but the matter rankled in her brain <\s>
<s> she could not bear sleeping dogs <\s>
<s> and there stirred in her a tortuous impulse to push the matter toward decision <\s>
<s> jon ought to be told so that either his feeling might be nipped in the bud or flowering in spite of the past come to fruition <\s>
<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>

<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>

<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>
<s> jolyon's native tenacity was roused and in the studio that evening he developed his objections <\s>
<s> he had never had any boils and his own teeth would last his time <\s>
<s> of course june admitted they would last his time if he didn't have them out <\s>
<s> but if he had more teeth he would have a better heart and his time would be longer <\s>
<s> his recalcitrance she said was a symptom of his whole attitude he was taking it lying down <\s>
<s> he ought to be fighting <\s>
<s> when was he going to see the man who had cured paul post <\s>
<s> jolyon was very sorry but the fact was he was not going to see him <\s>

<s> it was just such indifference and prejudice as her father manifested which was keeping him back <\s>
<s> it would be so splendid for both of them <\s>

<s> my dear it's the same thing <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>
<s> according to june it was foolish and even cowardly to hide the past from jon <\s>
<s> sheer opportunism she called it <\s>
<s> which jolyon put in mildly is the working principle of real life my dear <\s>
<s> cried june you don't really defend her for not telling jon dad <\s>
<s> if it were left to you you would <\s>
<s> i might but simply because i know he must find out which will be worse than if we told him <\s>
<s> then why don't you tell him <\s>
<s> it's just sleeping dogs again <\s>
<s> my dear said jolyon i wouldn't for the world go against irene's instinct <\s>
<s> yours too cried june <\s>
<s> what is a man's instinct compared with a mother's <\s>
<s> well i think it's very weak of you <\s>
<s> i dare say said jolyon i dare say <\s>
<s> and that was all she got from him but the matter rankled in her brain <\s>
<s> she could not bear sleeping dogs <\s>
<s> and there stirred in her a tortuous impulse to push the matter toward decision <\s>
<s> jon ought to be told so that either his feeling might be nipped in the bud or flowering in spite of the past come to fruition <\s>
<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>

<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>
<s> even genius itself attended these gatherings now and then with its nose on one side and june always introduced it to her father <\s>
<s> this she felt was exceptionally good for him for genius was a natural symptom he had never had fond as she was of him <\s>
<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>

<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>

<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>

<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>

<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>

<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>

<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>

<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>

<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>
<s> according to june it was foolish and even cowardly to hide the past from jon <\s>

<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>

<s> he had done wonders with <\s>

<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>
<s> even genius itself attended these gatherings now and then with its nose on one side and june always introduced it to her father <\s>
<s> this she felt was exceptionally good for him for genius was a natural symptom he had never had fond as she was of him <\s>
<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>
<s> jolyon's native tenacity was roused and in the studio that evening he developed his objections <\s>
<s> he had never had any boils and his own teeth would last his time <\s>
<s> of course june admitted they would last his time if he didn't have them out <\s>
<s> but if he had more teeth he would have a better heart and his time would be longer <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>
<s> even genius itself attended these gatherings now and then with its nose on one side and june always introduced it to her father <\s>
<s> this she felt was exceptionally good for him for genius was a natural symptom he had never had fond as she was of him <\s>
<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>
<s> jolyon's native tenacity was roused and in the studio that evening he developed his objections <\s>
<s> he had never had any boils and his own teeth would last his time <\s>
<s> of course june admitted they would last his time if he didn't have them out <\s>
<s> but if he had more teeth he would have a better heart and his time would be longer <\s>
<s> his recalcitrance she said was a symptom of his whole attitude he was taking it lying down <\s>
<s> he ought to be fighting <\s>
<s> when was he going to see the man who had cured paul post <\s>
<s> jolyon was very sorry but the fact was he was not going to see him <\s>
<s> pondridge she said the healer was such a fine man and he had such difficulty in making two ends meet and getting his theories recognised <\s>
<s> it was just such indifference and prejudice as her father manifested which was keeping him back <\s>
<s> it would be so splendid for both of them <\s>
<s> i perceive said jolyon that you are trying to kill two birds with one stone <\s>
<s> to cure you mean <\s>
<s> my dear it's the same thing <\s>
<s> it was unfair to say that without a trial <\s>
<s> jolyon thought he might not have the chance of saying it after <\s>

<s> that said jolyon is a fact but i wish to remain hopeless as long as possible <\s>

<s> they are quiet at present <\s>

<s> he puts his science before everything <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>

<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>
<s> according to june it was foolish and even cowardly to hide the past from jon <\s>

<s> jon ought to be told so that either his feeling might be nipped in the bud or flowering in spite of the past come to fruition <\s>
<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>
<s> he had made a special study of the symptoms of nature when his patient failed in any natural symptom he supplied the poison which caused it and there you were <\s>
<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>

<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>
<s> according to june it was foolish and even cowardly to hide the past from jon <\s>
<s> sheer opportunism she called it <\s>

<s> and that was all she got from him but the matter rankled in her brain <\s>
<s> she could not bear sleeping dogs <\s>
<s> and there stirred in her a tortuous impulse to push the matter toward decision <\s>
<s> jon ought to be told so that either his feeling might be nipped in the bud or flowering in spite of the past come to fruition <\s>
<s> and she determined to see fleur and judge for herself <\s>
<s> when june determined on anything delicacy became a somewhat minor consideration <\s>
<s> after all she was soames cousin and they were both interested in pictures <\s>
<s> she would go and tell him that he ought to buy a paul post or perhaps a piece of sculpture by boris strumolowski and of course she would say nothing to her father <\s>
<s> she went on the following sunday looking so determined that she had some difficulty in getting a cab at reading station <\s>
<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>
<s> she who had passed through this life without knowing what union was had a love of natural beauty which was almost madness <\s>
<s> and when she came to that choice spot where soames had pitched his tent she dismissed her cab because business over she wanted to revel in the bright water and the woods <\s>
<s> she appeared at his front door therefore as a mere pedestrian and sent in her card <\s>
<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>
<s> if one's nerves did not flutter she was taking the line of least resistance and knew that nobleness was not obliging her <\s>
<s> she was conducted to a drawing room which though not in her style showed every mark of fastidious elegance <\s>
<s> thinking too much taste too many knick knacks she saw in an old lacquer framed mirror the figure of a girl coming in from the verandah <\s>
<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
<s> through this device she still had twelve hundred a year and by reducing what she ate and in place of two belgians in a poor way employing one austrian in a poorer practically the same surplus for the relief of genius <\s>
<s> after three days at robin hill she carried her father back with her to town <\s>
<s> in those three days she had stumbled on the secret he had kept for two years and had instantly decided to cure him <\s>
<s> she knew in fact the very man <\s>
<s> he had done wonders with <\s>
<s> paul post that painter a little in advance of futurism and she was impatient with her father because his eyebrows would go up and because he had heard of neither <\s>
<s> of course if he hadn't faith he would never get well <\s>
<s> it was absurd not to have faith in the man who had healed paul post so that he had only just relapsed from having overworked or overlived himself again <\s>
<s> the great thing about this healer was that he relied on nature <\s>

<s> she was extremely hopeful <\s>
<s> her father had clearly not been living a natural life at robin hill and she intended to provide the symptoms <\s>
<s> he was she felt out of touch with the times which was not natural his heart wanted stimulating <\s>
<s> in the little chiswick house she and the austrian a grateful soul so devoted to june for rescuing her that she was in danger of decease from overwork stimulated jolyon in all sorts of ways preparing him for his cure <\s>
<s> but they could not keep his eyebrows down as for example when the austrian woke him at eight o'clock just as he was going to sleep or june took the times away from him because it was unnatural to read that stuff when he ought to be taking an interest in life <\s>
<s> he never failed indeed to be astonished at her resource especially in the evenings <\s>
<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>

<s> for his benefit as she declared though he suspected that she also got something out of it she assembled the age so far as it was satellite to genius and with some solemnity it would move up and down the studio before him in the fox trot and that more mental form of dancing the one step which so pulled against the music that jolyon's eyebrows would be almost lost in his hair from wonder at the strain it must impose on the dancer's will power <\s>
<s> aware that hung on the line in the water colour society he was a back number to those with any pretension to be called artists he would sit in the darkest corner he could find and wonder about rhythm on which so long ago he had been raised <\s>
<s> and when june brought some girl or young man up to him he would rise humbly to their level so far as that was possible and think dear me <\s>
<s> this is very dull for them <\s>
<s> having his father's perennial sympathy with youth he used to get very tired from entering into their points of view <\s>
<s> but it was all stimulating and he never failed in admiration of his daughter's indomitable spirit <\s>
<s> even genius itself attended these gatherings now and then with its nose on one side and june always introduced it to her father <\s>
<s> this she felt was exceptionally good for him for genius was a natural symptom he had never had fond as she was of him <\s>
<s> certain as a man can be that she was his own daughter he often wondered whence she got herself her red gold hair now greyed into a special colour her direct spirited face so different from his own rather folded and subtilised countenance her little lithe figure when he and most of the forsytes were tall <\s>
<s> and he would dwell on the origin of species and debate whether she might be danish or celtic <\s>
<s> celtic he thought from her pugnacity and her taste in fillets and djibbahs <\s>
<s> it was not too much to say that he preferred her to the age with which she was surrounded youthful though for the greater part it was <\s>
<s> she took however too much interest in his teeth for he still had some of those natural symptoms <\s>
<s> her dentist at once found staphylococcus aureus present in pure culture which might cause boils of course and wanted to take out all the teeth he had and supply him with two complete sets of unnatural symptoms <\s>

<s> he had never had any boils and his own teeth would last his time <\s>
<s> of course june admitted they would last his time if he didn't have them out <\s>
<s> but if he had more teeth he would have a better heart and his time would be longer <\s>

<s> june was silent having experienced in her time the inexorable character of her father's amiable obstinacy so far as his own freedom of action was concerned <\s>
<s> how he came to let her know why irene had taken jon to spain puzzled jolyon for he had little confidence in her discretion <\s>
<s> after she had brooded on the news it brought a rather sharp discussion during which he perceived to the full the fundamental opposition between her active temperament and his wife's passivity <\s>
<s> he even gathered that a little soreness still remained from that generation old struggle between them over the body of philip bosinney in which the passive had so signally triumphed over the active principle <\s>

<s> the river country was lovely in those days of her own month and june ached at its loveliness <\s>

<s> it was in june's character to know that when her nerves were fluttering she was doing something worth while <\s>

<s> clothed in white and holding some white roses in her hand she had reflected in that silvery grey pool of glass a vision like appearance as if a pretty ghost had come out of the green garden <\s>
